Note any fare class restrictions.\n- **Hotels**: compare at least one OTA vs. the hotel’s official site; include nightly rate, total with taxes/resort/parking fees, room type, cancellation deadline, location context (distance to target), review score, membership/AAA/corporate rates if applicable.\n- **Deals & promos**: look for official promo pages, loyalty/member rates, coupon fields. fallback to filename.\"\"\"\r\n    try:\r\n        raw = z.read(path).decode(\"utf-8\", errors=\"ignore\")\r\n    except KeyError:\r\n        return os.path.basename(path)\r\n    for line in raw.splitlines():\r\n        s = line.strip(\"\\ufeff\").strip()\r\n        if s.startswith(\"#\"):\r\n            # strip leading #'s\r\n            t = s.lstrip(\"#\").strip()\r\n            if t:\r\n                return t\r\n    # fallback: filename without extension\r\n    return os.path.splitext(os.path.basename(path))[0]\r\n\r\nlines = []\r\nlines.append(\"# Confluence Chronicles Story Bible — Master Index\")\r\nlines.append(\"\")\r\nlines.append(\"This file is the **master index** for the Confluence Chronicles Story Bible vault. \")\r\nlines.append(\"All major documents under `docs/` are linked below using relative paths so Obsidian can navigate the entire structure.\")\r\nlines.append(\"\")\r\n\r\n# Root files\r\nif root_files:\r\n    lines.append(\"## Root Files\")\r\n    for path in sorted(root_files):\r\n        title = get_title(path)\r\n        # Special-case common root files for nicer labels\r\n        if path == \"README.md\":\r\n            title = \"Confluence Chronicles — Story Bible (Repo Overview)\"\r\n        elif path.upper().startswith(\"CONTRIBUTING\"):\r\n            title = \"Contributing Guide\"\r\n        elif path.upper().startswith(\"CODE_OF_CONDUCT\"):\r\n            title = \"Code of Conduct\"\r\n        lines.append(f\"- [{title}]({path})\")\r\n    lines.append(\"\")\r\n\r\n# For docs/, build hierarchical headings based on path segments.\r\nlast_at_depth = {}\r\n\r\nfor path in sorted(docs_files):\r\n    parts = path.split(\"/\")\r\n    # parts[0] == \"docs\"\r\n    # depth index we care for headings: 1..len(parts)-2 are folders; last part is file\r\n    # For each folder depth, if changed, emit heading.\r\n    for depth in range(1, len(parts)-1):\r\n        key = (depth,)\r\n        folder_label = \"/\".join(parts[1:depth+1])\r\n        if last_at_depth.get(depth) != folder_label:\r\n            last_at_depth[depth] = folder_label\r\n            # Clear deeper levels\r\n            deeper = [d for d in list(last_at_depth.keys()) if d > depth]\r\n            for d in deeper:\r\n                del last_at_depth[d]\r\n            # Determine heading level: depth 1 -> ##, 2 -> ###, etc.\r\n            level = min(6, depth + 1)  # cap at h6 just in case\r\n            hashes = \"#\" * level\r\n            # Display label e.g. \"01-canon\" or \"04-plot / novellas\"\r\n            if depth == 1:\r\n                label = parts[depth]\r\n            else:\r\n                label = \" / \".join(parts[1:depth+1])\r\n            lines.append(f\"{hashes} {label}\")\r\n    # Now emit the file entry\r\n    title = get_title(path)\r\n    lines.append(f\"- [{title}]({path})\")\r\n\r\nindex_text = \"\\n\".join(lines)\r\n\r\nout_path = \"/mnt/data/ConfluenceChronicles-StoryBible-MASTER-INDEX-rebuilt.md\"\r\nwith open(out_path, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\r\n    f.write(index_text)\r\n\r\nout_path[:120], index_text.splitlines()[:40]"

Tooling enforces **lexicon**, **knowledge gates**, and **cost visibility**.\n\n## Quick Start\n- Browse `/docs` first.\n- See `/docs/01-canon/` for **Master Lexicon**, **Magic System Production Canon**, and **N01–N05 Knowledge Gates & Scene Ladder**.\n- Use `make lint` (or run the Python scripts in `tools/lint/`) to check lexicon and era redlines.\n- Open `.github/workflows/ci.yml` for the CI that runs the custom linters in PRs.\n\n## Structure\n```\ndocs/\n  00-overview/\n  01-canon/\n  02-world/\n  03-characters/\n  04-plot/\n    turnings/\n    meta/\n  05-ops/\ntools/\n  lint/\n  templates/\n.github/\n  ISSUE_TEMPLATE/\n  workflows/\n```\n- **Canon**: rules you can’t break.  \n- **World/Characters**: reference.  \n- **Plot**: turning/novella outlines and met\n"

            "#!/usr/bin/env python3\nimport os, json, re, argparse, glob, hashlib\n\ndef read_text(path):\n    try:\n        return open(path, \"r\", encoding=\"utf-8\", errors=\"ignore\").read()\n    except:\n        return \"\"\n\ndef chunk_text(text, max_chars=1800, overlap=200):\n    chunks = []\n    start = 0\n    n = len(text)\n    while start < n:\n        end = min(n, start + max_chars)\n        cut = text.rfind(\"\\n\\n\", start, end)\n        if cut == -1 or cut <= start + 200:\n            cut = end\n        chunks.append(text[start:cut])\n        start = max(cut - overlap, cut)\n    return [c for c in chunks if c.strip()]\n\ndef path_tags(path):\n    tags = []\n    p = path.replace(\"\\\\\", \"/\")\n    m = re.search(r\"/novellas/(N\\d{2})\", p)\n    if m: tags.append(m.group(1))\n    if \"/01-canon/\" in p: tags.append(\"canon\")\n    if \"/05-ops/\" in p: tags.append(\"ops\")\n    return tags\n\ndef main():\n    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()\n    ap.add_argument(\"--roots\", nargs=\"+\", default=[\"docs/01-canon\",\"docs/04-plot/novellas\",\"docs/05-ops\"])\n    ap.add_argument(\"--out\", default=\"ai/index/index.jsonl\")\n    ap.add_argument(\"--max-chars\", type=int, default=1800)\n    ap.add_argument(\"--overlap\", type=int, default=200)\n    args = ap.parse_args()\n\n    records = []\n    for root in args.roots:\n        for path in glob.glob(os.path.join(root, \"**\", \"*.*\"), recursive=True):\n            if not path.lower().endswith((\".md\",\".txt\")): continue\n            if not os.path.isfile(path): continue\n            txt = read_text(path)\n            for i, ch in enumerate(chunk_text(txt, args.max_chars, args.overlap)):\n                rid = hashlib.md5(f\"{path}:{i}\".encode()).hexdigest()\n                rec = {\"id\":rid, \"path\":path.replace(\"\\\\\",\"/\"), \"chunk_id\":i, \"text\":ch, \"tags\":path_tags(path)}\n                records.append(rec)\n\n    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(args.out), exist_ok=True)\n    with open(args.out, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        for r in records:\n            f.write(json.dumps(r, ensure_ascii=False)+\"\\n\")\n    print(f\"Wrote {len(records)} chunks to {args.out}\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n"

create folder headings for each level under docs\r\n    for depth in range(1, len(parts)-1):\r\n        folder_label = \"/\".join(parts[1:depth+1])\r\n        if last_at_depth.get(depth) != folder_label:\r\n            last_at_depth[depth] = folder_label\r\n            # clear deeper levels to avoid mixing branches\r\n            deeper = [d for d in list(last_at_depth.keys()) if d > depth]\r\n            for d in deeper:\r\n                del last_at_depth[d]\r\n            level = min(6, depth + 1)  # h2 for top-level under docs\r\n            hashes = \"#\" * level\r\n            if depth == 1:\r\n                label = parts[depth]\r\n            else:\r\n                label = \" / \".join(parts[1:depth+1])\r\n            lines.append(f\"{hashes} {label}\")\r\n    title = get_title(path)\r\n    lines.append(f\"- [{title}]({path})\")\r\n\r\nindex_text = \"\\n\".join(lines)\r\nlen(index_text.splitlines()), index_text[:1000]",
